***ooit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ooit.html>ooit</a> (250)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">oit</i>. The further etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not clear, as there are no parallels in other languages. Possibly a combination of Old Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">io</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*jit</i> (cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:jetzt.html>jetzt</a></i> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ġiet</i> gt; Modern English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">yet</i>), although this leaves the initial <i>o-</i> unexplained.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ooit.html>ooit</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>sometime (in the future)
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ooit.html>ooit</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heen.html>heen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a></i>
<dl><dd>I will go around there <b>sometime in the future</b></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>ever
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ooit.html>ooit</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:getennist.html>getennist</a>?</i>
<dl><dd>have you <b>ever</b> played tennis?</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>once (in the past)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>Zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:miste.html>miste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ooit.html>ooit</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> NK <a href = vnd.unilang:dammen.html>dammen</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:utrecht.html>Utrecht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:omdat.html>omdat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:trein.html>trein</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:slaap.html>slaap</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gevallen.html>gevallen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enkele.html>enkele</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:keren.html>keren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tussen.html>tussen</a> Groningen <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zwellen.html>Zwolle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heen.html>heen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gereden.html>gereden</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>So <b>once</b> he missed the NK <a href = vnd.unilang:checkers.html>checkers</a> [tournament] in <a href = vnd.unilang:utrecht.html>Utrecht</a> because he <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> fallen asleep in the train and <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> ridden a few times back and forth between Groningen and <a href = vnd.unilang:zwellen.html>Zwolle</a>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ook.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> (61)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ôoc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ōk</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ouk</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*auk</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>also, too, moreover
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I can do that too.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mentale.html>Mentale</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gezondheid.html>gezondheid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gezondheid.html>gezondheid</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Mental health <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also health.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in negative sentences</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> either
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I can'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> do that either.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>-ever
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>wie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a></b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">whoever</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a></b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">wherever</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>particle for emphasis
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geduurd.html>geduurd</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> take very long.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***oor.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:oor.html>oor</a> (2357)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ore</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ōra</i>, from the voiced Verner alternant of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ausô</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂ows-</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Ohr</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">ear</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ear</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">øre</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oor.html>oor</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oren.html>oren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oortje.html>oortje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>ear</li>
<li>handle (of cup, mug)</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***oordeel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:oordeel.html>oordeel</a> (3318)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ordeel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">urdēl</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*uzdailiją</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">oor-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deel.html>deel</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Urteil</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ordeal</i>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">ordeal</span>.
</p>

***oorlog.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:oorlog.html>oorlog</a> (513)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">orloge</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*urlage</i>. In this word, two Germanic <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> merged, both having the prefix <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ur-</i> (modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oor.html>oor</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oer.html>oer</a></i>, with the former kept in compounds like <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oorzaak.html>oorzaak</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cause, driver</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oorsprong.html>oorsprong</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">origin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and the latter borrowed from German). The first word <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*uzlagą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fate, destiny</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laga-</i> related to modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leggen.html>leggen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to lay</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The second word <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*uzleugō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">war</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*leug-</i> meaning “oath”.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oorlog.html>oorlog</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oorlogen.html>oorlogen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oorlogje.html>oorlogje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">war</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***oorlogsverleden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:oorlogsverleden.html>oorlogsverleden</a> (59781)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1917 in relation to the replacement of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Theobald_von_Bethmann-Hollweg" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Theobald von Bethmann-Hollweg">Theobald von Bethmann-Hollweg</a> with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Georg_Michaelis" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Georg Michaelis">Georg Michaelis</a>. Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oorlog.html>oorlog</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">war</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verleden.html>verleden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">past</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kriegsvergangenheit</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oorlogsverleden.html>oorlogsverleden</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oorlogsverleden.html>oorlogsverledens</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>wartime past, past relating to a war
<ul><li><b>1917</b> July 16, "<a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> kanselierswisseling in Duitsland", <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Maasbode</i>, page 1, quoting the "Börsencourier" (only in translation).
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>Zijn</a> werkzaamheid <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:buiten.html>buiten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ziek.html>ziek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:giften.html>giften</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:oorlogsverleden.html>oorlogsverleden</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">His activity involving foreign nations <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not afflicted by poisons of the <b>wartime past</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Very often associated with negative connotations, often used euphemistically for a past that involved atrocities or association with e.g. Nazis.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:oorlogsverleden.html>oorlogsverleden</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vroeger.html>vroeger</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oorlog.html>oorlog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebeurd.html>gebeurd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedaan.html>gedaan</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:meegemaakt.html>meegemaakt</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oorlog.html>oorlog</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i> Stanton <a href = vnd.unilang:vertelde.html>vertelde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verhaal.html>verhaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> ‘<a href = vnd.unilang:gewone.html>gewone</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a>’, <a href = vnd.unilang:zonder.html>zonder</a> <a href = <p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oor.html>oor</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vijg.html>vijg</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fig</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unclear whether <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">oorvaag</i> etc. developed independently, from <i><a href = vnd.unilang:oor.html>oor</a></i> + the root of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vegen.html>vegen</a></i>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vagen.html>vagen</a></i> 'to wipe', or are popular etymology from the older <i><a href = vnd.unilang:oorvijg.html>oorvijg</a></i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> Germanic cognates, including German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Ohrfeige</i>, and similar vegetal-manual semantics such as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">vuistlook</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fist garlic</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:oost.html>oost</a> (5869)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:oost.html>oost</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ōst</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*austrą</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:ost.html>Ost</a></i>, English and West Frisian <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">east</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">aust</i>. Doublet of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oosten.html>oosten</a></i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">only in compounds</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> east
<dl><dd><i>Oost-Berlijn</i>  |  East Berlin</dd></dl></li>
<li>eastwards</li></ol>

***op.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> (19)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">up</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*upp</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stuiterde.html>stuiterde</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:neer.html>neer</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The ball bounced <b>up</b> and down.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">postpositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> onto, up onto
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kat.html>kat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klom.html>klom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gisteren.html>gisteren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dak.html>dak</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The cat climbed <b>onto</b> the roof yesterday.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">Used in separative verbs meaning “to go away” with rude connotations.</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_4">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>on, upon
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:melk.html>melk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:staat.html>staat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tafel.html>tafel</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The milk <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>on</b> the table.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> ... <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></span><span class="ib-comma">,</span> with a cardinal number</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a>, except <span class="use-with-mention">Used to form ordinal numbers in relation to a superlative quality. <p>Probably borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">opale</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">opalus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὀπάλλιος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">opállios</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">उपल</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">upala</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***opal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:opal.html>opal</a> (17612)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>In Florio’s <i>A World of <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>Words</a></i> 1598 as <i>opale</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">opale</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">opalus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὀπάλλιος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">opállios</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">उपल</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">upala</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gem, stone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">उपरि</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">upári</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the upper millstone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:opal.html>opal</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">opals</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mineralogy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A mineral consisting, like quartz, of silica, but inferior to quartz in hardness and specific gravity, of the chemical formula SiO<sub>2</sub><b>·</b>NH<sub>2</sub><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b> March 1,  Lee A. Groat,  “Gemstones”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_Scientist" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:American Scientist">American Scientist</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.americanscientist.org/issues/feature/2012/2/gemstones">[1]</a></sup>, volume 100, number 2, page 128:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Although there are dozens of different <a href = vnd.unilang:types.html>types</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:gems.html>gems</a>, among the <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> known and most important are [ | ] | . (Common gem materials not addressed in this article include <a href = vnd.unilang:amber.html>amber</a>, amethyst, chalcedony, garnet, lazurite, malachite, <b>opals</b>, peridot, rhodonite, spinel, tourmaline, <a href = vnd.unilang:turquoise.html>turquoise</a> and zircon.)</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology<span class="ib-comma">,</span> genetics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> biochemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A colloquial name used in molecular biology referring to a particular <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a> codon sequence, "UGA."</li>
<li>Any of various lycaenid butterflies of the genus <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Nesolycaena" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Nesolycaena"><i>Nesolycaena</i></a></span>.</li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:opdracht.html>opdracht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">swelling, transfer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opdracht.html>opdracht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opdrachten.html>opdrachten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opdracht.html>opdrachtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>task, an action that one <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> required to do</li>
<li>commission, something that <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> commissioned</li>
<li>order, request</li>
<li>dedication (handwritten, by author)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> transfer (of possessions, etc.)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A swelling, a rash.</li></ol>

<ol><li>to appear, to emerge, to turn up, to show up (usually suddenly after being hidden or absent for some time)</li>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">at</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">once</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
